Natürlich war das Unsinn, aber der Eingeborene sah nicht wie ein Mann aus, der zu idiotischen Scherzen fähig war - es war wahrscheinlicher, dass ihm jemand einen sehr grausamen Scherz gespielt hatte. Warum sollte man das nicht überprüfen?

#QUEST DTSG
Long Shadows of Old Sins
#TEXT   1
Warum passieren mir immer solche Zufälle? Gerade als Charlie und ich unsere Pfeifen befeuchten und eine Pause von der Hitze der Straße machen wollten, wurden wir in der Taverne überfallen. Das Interessanteste daran war, dass sich die Aufmerksamkeit des Unruhestifters nicht einmal auf mich richtete, sondern auf Charlie.

Es lohnt sich wahrscheinlich, das Schloss zu finden, das zu dem Schlüssel passt, den ich in der Tasche dieses Schurken gefunden habe.
#TEXT   2

Now I have to fight on Peter's behalf in a duel in a couple of hours just outside the city. I'm not against helping those in need who deserve it. But I need to have a serious talk with Charlie afterwards, to make sure he never makes decisions for me again.

#QUEST TheFormerKnight
Former Knight of the Order
#TEXT   1
No sooner had I stepped into the tavern than I was approached by my officer, Claude Durand. At first, I thought the scoundrel would ask for money, as usual, but the matter turned out to be far more serious. He owes Levasseur a favor and fears that failure to fulfill it could cost him his life. The favor is a grim one: to track down and kill a former Knight of the Order of Malta whose name is unknown to us. He`s hiding in one of the English colonies. Durand's sword, strength, and skill are valuable to me, and he offers his loyalty in return. I agreed to help him, but even if we manage to find this needle in a haystack, the fight with this man definitely will be no easy task.
#TEXT   2
We managed to track down and eliminate the former Knight of the Order. Durand was intent on killing the knight's woman, who was unfortunate enough to be in the house at the time. Fortunately, I managed to reason with him. It's unsettling to realize he was capable of such an act, but I've spoken with him and am confident that under my command, he won't entertain such thoughts anymore.
#TEXT   3
We managed to track down and eliminate the former Knight of the Order. Unfortunately, his woman happened to be in the house as well. Durand killed her too. I am partly to blame for this myself. I'm not thrilled by such actions, but it's part of his work and his past. Now he is free of his debt, and I hope he will remain loyal to me.
#TEXT   4
We managed to track down and eliminate the former Knight of the Order. Durand was intent on killing the knight's woman, who was unfortunate enough to be in the house at the time. Naturally, I couldn't allow this. We crossed swords once again, and once again, I proved stronger. Had I known earlier what a scoundrel he was, I would have ended him back at Levasseur's residence.

#QUEST Tichingitu
Tichingitu
#TEXT   1
After Fadey was robbed, another robber broke into his place. It was an Indian, apparently in war paint. Fadey managed to detain him and handed the thief over to the commandant. I've heard so much about them, but I've never seen an Indian in real life. Since fate has thrown me into the New World, why not get to know this native better? After all, they are an important part of this world.
#TEXT   2
I visited the Indian who broke into Fadey's house. His name is Tichingitu. He saia he had come to town looking food. The punishment Fadey and the commandant have in store for him seems rather harsh. I should discuss it with the prison warden. Perhaps I can convince him to lessen the sentence.
#TEXT   3
For a handful of gold doubloons, Fadey showed magnanimity and agreed to pardon the Indian. The commandant has no objections to this arrangement, and I can now inform Tichingitu that he is free.
#TEXT   4
The Indian expressed a desire to join my crew. After some brief consideration I agreed. A loyal bodyguard who knows his way around a musket will undoubtedly be useful.
#TEXT   5
The Indian, impressed by my selfless rescue of his skin from the grip of justice, persistently asked to join my crew as a bodyguard. I refused him. I am afraid that the presence of an unbaptized savage in the crew would cause a negative reaction among the men.
#TEXT   6
I didn't go to the Indian in prison. He has probably been already hanged.
